KLIFS

Structural Bioinformatics
Parsing Kinase strutures information from KLIFS
Author

Samdani Ansar

Published

May 21, 2023

In this post we will see how to use KLIFS API and different information which we can be fetched and analysed.

  • All the API point functionality
  • Use case 1 For a given ligand fetch all the x-ray stractures, examine the conformational states and their IC50 value.
    • if different kinase conformations check for the ligand pose
    • if same kinase conformations check for interaction with conserved site
#@title *Install PLIP**
!conda install -c conda-forge plip -y
from plip.basic import config
from plip.structure.preparation import PDBComplex
from plip.exchange.report import BindingSiteReport
import pandas as pd

API points

https://github.com/volkamerlab/opencadd/blob/master/opencadd/databases/klifs/remote.py#L34

https://bravado.readthedocs.io/en/stable/quickstart.html

https://klifs.net/swagger_v2/

from bravado.client import SwaggerClient

KLIFS_API = SwaggerClient.from_url(
    "https://dev.klifs.net/swagger_v2/swagger.json", config={"validate_responses": False}
)
KLIFS_API.swagger_spec.spec_dict.keys()
dict_keys(['swagger', 'info', 'host', 'schemes', 'basePath', 'produces', 'paths', 'definitions'])
KLIFS_API.swagger_spec.spec_dict['paths']['/kinase_names']['get'].keys()
dict_keys(['summary', 'description', 'tags', 'parameters', 'responses'])
KLIFS_API.swagger_spec.spec_dict['paths']['/kinase_names']['get']['parameters']
[{'name': 'kinase_group',
  'in': 'query',
  'description': 'Optional: Name or list of names of the kinase group for which the kinase families are requested (e.g. TKL,STE).',
  'required': False,
  'type': 'array',
  'items': {'type': 'string'}},
 {'name': 'kinase_family',
  'in': 'query',
  'description': 'Optional: Name list of names of the kinase family for which the kinase names are requested (e.g. AUR,WEE).',
  'required': False,
  'type': 'array',
  'items': {'type': 'string'}},
 {'name': 'species',
  'in': 'query',
  'description': 'Optional: Species for which the kinase names are requested (e.g. HUMAN OR MOUSE).',
  'required': False,
  'type': 'string'}]
KLIFS_API.swagger_spec.spec_dict['definitions'].keys()
dict_keys(['structureDetails', 'ligandDetails', 'IFPList', 'InteractionList', 'MatchList', 'IDlist', 'ModifiedResiduesList', 'KinaseInformation', 'BioactivityDetails', 'DrugDetails', 'ConformationDetails', 'Error'])
paths = KLIFS_API.swagger_spec.spec_dict['paths']
for path, path_definition in paths.items():
    for method, method_definition in path_definition.items():
        responses = method_definition.get('responses', {})
        for response_code, response_definition in responses.items():
            if 'schema' in response_definition:
                schema = response_definition['schema']
                if '$ref' in schema:
                    ref_value = schema['$ref']
                    print("Path:", path)
                    print("Method:", method)
                    print("Response Code:", response_code)
                    print("$ref Value:", ref_value)
